ant-btn-icon-only" style="background-color:#f18f01;border-color:#f18f01"><span class="ant-btn-icon"><span role="img" aria-label="warning" class="anticon anticon-warning"><svg viewBox="64 64 896 896" focusable="false" data-icon="warning" width="1em" height="1em" fill="currentColor" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M464 720a48 48 0 1096 0 48 48 0 10-96 0zm16-304v184c0 4.4 3.6 8 8 8h48c4.4 0 8-3.6 8-8V416c0-4.4-3.6-8-8-8h-48c-4.4 0-8 3.6-8 8zm475.7 440l-416-720c-6.2-10.7-16.9-16-27.7-16s-21.6 5.3-27.7 16l-416 720C56 877.4 71.4 904 96 904h832c24.6 0 40-26.6 27.7-48zm-783.5-27.9L512 239.9l339.8 588.2H172.2z"></path></svg></span></span></button></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="ant-col ant-col-24 css-3uaqrl css-var-_R_6_"><div class="fullscreen"><div class="ant-card ant-card-bordered css-3uaqrl css-var-_R_6_" style="max-height:100%;overflow-y:auto"><div class="ant-card-body"><p>You mainly want <strong>the authentication API flow and how the PASETO token is obtained</strong>, separated from the React/wallet code. I’ll simplify the <strong>actual backend interaction steps</strong> used in your code.</p>
<p>Your authentication flow is basically:</p>
<pre><code node="[object Object]">Wallet Connect
     ↓
Get Flow ID + EULA
     ↓
User signs message with wallet
     ↓
Send signature to authenticate API
     ↓
Receive PASETO token
     ↓
Store token in cookie
</code></pre>
<p>Below is the <strong>clean extracted API process</strong>.</p>
<hr/>
<h1>1. Get Authentication Flow (FlowID API)</h1>
<h3>Request</h3>
<pre><code node="[object Object]">GET /api/v1.0/flowid
</code></pre>
<h3>Query Parameters</h3>
<table><thead><tr><th>Parameter</th><th>Example</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>walletAddress</td><td>0xabc...</td><td>User wallet address</td></tr><tr><td>chain</td><td>evm / sol</td><td>Blockchain type</td></tr></tbody></table>
<h3>Example</h3>
<pre><div node="[object Object]" style="background:hsl(220, 13%, 18%);color:hsl(220, 14%, 71%);text-shadow:0 1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3);font-family:&quot;Fira Code&quot;, &quot;Fira Mono&quot;, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;DejaVu Sans Mono&quot;, monospace;direction:ltr;text-align:left;white-space:pre;word-spacing:normal;word-break:normal;line-height:1.5;-moz-tab-size:2;-o-tab-size:2;tab-size:2;-webkit-hyphens:none;-moz-hyphens:none;-ms-hyphens:none;hyphens:none;padding:1em;margin:0.5em 0;overflow:auto;border-radius:0.3em"><code class="language-http" style="white-space:pre;background:hsl(220, 13%, 18%);color:hsl(220, 14%, 71%);text-shadow:0 1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3);font-family:&quot;Fira Code&quot;, &quot;Fira Mono&quot;, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;DejaVu Sans Mono&quot;, monospace;direction:ltr;text-align:left;word-spacing:normal;word-break:normal;line-height:1.5;-moz-tab-size:2;-o-tab-size:2;tab-size:2;-webkit-hyphens:none;-moz-hyphens:none;-ms-hyphens:none;hyphens:none">GET https://gateway.netsepio.com/api/v1.0/flowid?walletAddress=0xabc123&amp;chain=evm</code></div></pre>
<h3>Response</h3>
<pre><div node="[object Object]" style="background:hsl(220, 13%, 18%);color:hsl(220, 14%, 71%);text-shadow:0 1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3);font-family:&quot;Fira Code&quot;, &quot;Fira Mono&quot;, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;DejaVu Sans Mono&quot;, monospace;direction:ltr;text-align:left;white-space:pre;word-spacing:normal;word-break:normal;line-height:1.5;-moz-tab-size:2;-o-tab-size:2;tab-size:2;-webkit-hyphens:none;-moz-hyphens:none;-ms-hyphens:none;hyphens:none;padding:1em;margin:0.5em 0;overflow:auto;border-radius:0.3em"><code class="language-json" style="white-space:pre;background:hsl(220, 13%, 18%);color:hsl(220, 14%, 71%);text-shadow:0 1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3);font-family:&quot;Fira Code&quot;, &quot;Fira Mono&quot;, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;DejaVu Sans Mono&quot;, monospace;direction:ltr;text-align:left;word-spacing:normal;word-break:normal;line-height:1.5;-moz-tab-size:2;-o-tab-size:2;tab-size:2;-webkit-hyphens:none;-moz-hyphens:none;-ms-hyphens:none;hyphens:none">{
  &quot;payload&quot;: {
    &quot;flowId&quot;: &quot;FLOW_ID&quot;,
    &quot;eula&quot;: &quot;Terms and conditions message&quot;
  }
}</code></div></pre>
<h3>Purpose</h3>
<p>This returns:</p>
<pre><code node="[object Object]">flowId → authentication session
eula → message that user must sign
</code></pre>
<hr/>
<h1>2. Prepare Message to Sign</h1>
<p>Your code does this:</p>
<pre><div node="[object Object]" style="background:hsl(220, 13%, 18%);color:hsl(220, 14%, 71%);text-shadow:0 1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3);font-family:&quot;Fira Code&quot;, &quot;Fira Mono&quot;, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;DejaVu Sans Mono&quot;, monospace;direction:ltr;text-align:left;white-space:pre;word-spacing:normal;word-break:normal;line-height:1.5;-moz-tab-size:2;-o-tab-size:2;tab-size:2;-webkit-hyphens:none;-moz-hyphens:none;-ms-hyphens:none;hyphens:none;padding:1em;margin:0.5em 0;overflow:auto;border-radius:0.3em"><code class="language-text" style="white-space:pre;background:hsl(220, 13%, 18%);color:hsl(220, 14%, 71%);text-shadow:0 1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3);font-family:&quot;Fira Code&quot;, &quot;Fira Mono&quot;, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;DejaVu Sans Mono&quot;, monospace;direction:ltr;text-align:left;word-spacing:normal;word-break:normal;line-height:1.5;-moz-tab-size:2;-o-tab-size:2;tab-size:2;-webkit-hyphens:none;-moz-hyphens:none;-ms-hyphens:none;hyphens:none">const combinedMessage = `${normalizedMessage}${flowId}`;</code></div></pre>
<p>Example message:</p>
<pre><code node="[object Object]">CyreneAI Terms and Conditions...
FLOW_ID
</code></pre>
<p>This message is signed by the wallet.</p>
<hr/>
<h1>3. User Signs Message</h1>
<h3>EVM Wallet</h3>
<pre><div node="[object Object]" style="background:hsl(220, 13%, 18%);color:hsl(220, 14%, 71%);text-shadow:0 1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3);font-family:&quot;Fira Code&quot;, &quot;Fira Mono&quot;, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;DejaVu Sans Mono&quot;, monospace;direction:ltr;text-align:left;white-space:pre;word-spacing:normal;word-break:normal;line-height:1.5;-moz-tab-size:2;-o-tab-size:2;tab-size:2;-webkit-hyphens:none;-moz-hyphens:none;-ms-hyphens:none;hyphens:none;padding:1em;margin:0.5em 0;overflow:auto;border-radius:0.3em"><code class="language-text" style="white-space:pre;background:hsl(220, 13%, 18%);color:hsl(220, 14%, 71%);text-shadow:0 1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3);font-family:&quot;Fira Code&quot;, &quot;Fira Mono&quot;, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;DejaVu Sans Mono&quot;, monospace;direction:ltr;text-align:left;word-spacing:normal;word-break:normal;line-height:1.5;-moz-tab-size:2;-o-tab-size:2;tab-size:2;-webkit-hyphens:none;-moz-hyphens:none;-ms-hyphens:none;hyphens:none">const signature = await signer.signMessage(combinedMessage);</code></div></pre>
<p>Result example:</p>
<pre><code node="[object Object]">0x9f32c1ab...
</code></pre>
<p>Then your code removes <code node="[object Object]">0x</code>.</p>
<hr/>
<h3>Solana Wallet</h3>
<pre><div node="[object Object]" style="background:hsl(220, 13%, 18%);color:hsl(220, 14%, 71%);text-shadow:0 1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3);font-family:&quot;Fira Code&quot;, &quot;Fira Mono&quot;, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;DejaVu Sans Mono&quot;, monospace;direction:ltr;text-align:left;white-space:pre;word-spacing:normal;word-break:normal;line-height:1.5;-moz-tab-size:2;-o-tab-size:2;tab-size:2;-webkit-hyphens:none;-moz-hyphens:none;-ms-hyphens:none;hyphens:none;padding:1em;margin:0.5em 0;overflow:auto;border-radius:0.3em"><code class="language-text" style="white-space:pre;background:hsl(220, 13%, 18%);color:hsl(220, 14%, 71%);text-shadow:0 1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3);font-family:&quot;Fira Code&quot;, &quot;Fira Mono&quot;, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;DejaVu Sans Mono&quot;, monospace;direction:ltr;text-align:left;word-spacing:normal;word-break:normal;line-height:1.5;-moz-tab-size:2;-o-tab-size:2;tab-size:2;-webkit-hyphens:none;-moz-hyphens:none;-ms-hyphens:none;hyphens:none">const encodedMessage = new TextEncoder().encode(normalizedMessage);
const signature = await walletProvider.signMessage(encodedMessage);</code></div></pre>
<p>Converted to hex:</p>
<pre><div node="[object Object]" style="background:hsl(220, 13%, 18%);color:hsl(220, 14%, 71%);text-shadow:0 1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3);font-family:&quot;Fira Code&quot;, &quot;Fira Mono&quot;, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;DejaVu Sans Mono&quot;, monospace;direction:ltr;text-align:left;white-space:pre;word-spacing:normal;word-break:normal;line-height:1.5;-moz-tab-size:2;-o-tab-size:2;tab-size:2;-webkit-hyphens:none;-moz-hyphens:none;-ms-hyphens:none;hyphens:none;padding:1em;margin:0.5em 0;overflow:auto;border-radius:0.3em"><code class="language-text" style="white-space:pre;background:hsl(220, 13%, 18%);color:hsl(220, 14%, 71%);text-shadow:0 1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3);font-family:&quot;Fira Code&quot;, &quot;Fira Mono&quot;, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;DejaVu Sans Mono&quot;, monospace;direction:ltr;text-align:left;word-spacing:normal;word-break:normal;line-height:1.5;-moz-tab-size:2;-o-tab-size:2;tab-size:2;-webkit-hyphens:none;-moz-hyphens:none;-ms-hyphens:none;hyphens:none">const signatureHex = ...</code></div></pre>
<hr/>
<h1>4. Authenticate API (Generate PASETO Token)</h1>
<h3>Request</h3>
<pre><code node="[object Object]">POST /api/v1.0/authenticate
</code></pre>
<hr/>
<h2>EVM Example</h2>
<pre><div node="[object Object]" style="background:hsl(220, 13%, 18%);color:hsl(220, 14%, 71%);text-shadow:0 1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3);font-family:&quot;Fira Code&quot;, &quot;Fira Mono&quot;, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;DejaVu Sans Mono&quot;, monospace;direction:ltr;text-align:left;white-space:pre;word-spacing:normal;word-break:normal;line-height:1.5;-moz-tab-size:2;-o-tab-size:2;tab-size:2;-webkit-hyphens:none;-moz-hyphens:none;-ms-hyphens:none;hyphens:none;padding:1em;margin:0.5em 0;overflow:auto;border-radius:0.3em"><code class="language-http" style="white-space:pre;background:hsl(220, 13%, 18%);color:hsl(220, 14%, 71%);text-shadow:0 1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3);font-family:&quot;Fira Code&quot;, &quot;Fira Mono&quot;, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;DejaVu Sans Mono&quot;, monospace;direction:ltr;text-align:left;word-spacing:normal;word-break:normal;line-height:1.5;-moz-tab-size:2;-o-tab-size:2;tab-size:2;-webkit-hyphens:none;-moz-hyphens:none;-ms-hyphens:none;hyphens:none">POST https://gateway.netsepio.com/api/v1.0/authenticate</code></div></pre>
<p>Body</p>
<pre><div node="[object Object]" style="background:hsl(220, 13%, 18%);color:hsl(220, 14%, 71%);text-shadow:0 1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3);font-family:&quot;Fira Code&quot;, &quot;Fira Mono&quot;, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;DejaVu Sans Mono&quot;, monospace;direction:ltr;text-align:left;white-space:pre;word-spacing:normal;word-break:normal;line-height:1.5;-moz-tab-size:2;-o-tab-size:2;tab-size:2;-webkit-hyphens:none;-moz-hyphens:none;-ms-hyphens:none;hyphens:none;padding:1em;margin:0.5em 0;overflow:auto;border-radius:0.3em"><code class="language-json" style="white-space:pre;background:hsl(220, 13%, 18%);color:hsl(220, 14%, 71%);text-shadow:0 1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3);font-family:&quot;Fira Code&quot;, &quot;Fira Mono&quot;, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;DejaVu Sans Mono&quot;, monospace;direction:ltr;text-align:left;word-spacing:normal;word-break:normal;line-height:1.5;-moz-tab-size:2;-o-tab-size:2;tab-size:2;-webkit-hyphens:none;-moz-hyphens:none;-ms-hyphens:none;hyphens:none">{
  &quot;chainName&quot;: &quot;evm&quot;,
  &quot;flowId&quot;: &quot;FLOW_ID&quot;,
  &quot;signature&quot;: &quot;SIGNATURE_WITHOUT_0x&quot;,
  &quot;walletAddress&quot;: &quot;0xabc123&quot;
}</code></div></pre>
<hr/>
<h2>Solana Example</h2>
<pre><div node="[object Object]" style="background:hsl(220, 13%, 18%);color:hsl(220, 14%, 71%);text-shadow:0 1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3);font-family:&quot;Fira Code&quot;, &quot;Fira Mono&quot;, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;DejaVu Sans Mono&quot;, monospace;direction:ltr;text-align:left;white-space:pre;word-spacing:normal;word-break:normal;line-height:1.5;-moz-tab-size:2;-o-tab-size:2;tab-size:2;-webkit-hyphens:none;-moz-hyphens:none;-ms-hyphens:none;hyphens:none;padding:1em;margin:0.5em 0;overflow:auto;border-radius:0.3em"><code class="language-http" style="white-space:pre;background:hsl(220, 13%, 18%);color:hsl(220, 14%, 71%);text-shadow:0 1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3);font-family:&quot;Fira Code&quot;, &quot;Fira Mono&quot;, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;DejaVu Sans Mono&quot;, monospace;direction:ltr;text-align:left;word-spacing:normal;word-break:normal;line-height:1.5;-moz-tab-size:2;-o-tab-size:2;tab-size:2;-webkit-hyphens:none;-moz-hyphens:none;-ms-hyphens:none;hyphens:none">POST https://gateway.netsepio.com/api/v1.0/authenticate?walletAddress=SOLANA_ADDRESS&amp;chain=sol</code></div></pre>
<p>Body</p>
<pre><div node="[object Object]" style="background:hsl(220, 13%, 18%);color:hsl(220, 14%, 71%);text-shadow:0 1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3);font-family:&quot;Fira Code&quot;, &quot;Fira Mono&quot;, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;DejaVu Sans Mono&quot;, monospace;direction:ltr;text-align:left;white-space:pre;word-spacing:normal;word-break:normal;line-height:1.5;-moz-tab-size:2;-o-tab-size:2;tab-size:2;-webkit-hyphens:none;-moz-hyphens:none;-ms-hyphens:none;hyphens:none;padding:1em;margin:0.5em 0;overflow:auto;border-radius:0.3em"><code class="language-json" style="white-space:pre;background:hsl(220, 13%, 18%);color:hsl(220, 14%, 71%);text-shadow:0 1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3);font-family:&quot;Fira Code&quot;, &quot;Fira Mono&quot;, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;DejaVu Sans Mono&quot;, monospace;direction:ltr;text-align:left;word-spacing:normal;word-break:normal;line-height:1.5;-moz-tab-size:2;-o-tab-size:2;tab-size:2;-webkit-hyphens:none;-moz-hyphens:none;-ms-hyphens:none;hyphens:none">{
  &quot;flowId&quot;: &quot;FLOW_ID&quot;,
  &quot;signature&quot;: &quot;HEX_SIGNATURE&quot;,
  &quot;pubKey&quot;: &quot;SOLANA_ADDRESS&quot;,
  &quot;walletAddress&quot;: &quot;SOLANA_ADDRESS&quot;,
  &quot;message&quot;: &quot;SIGNED_MESSAGE&quot;,
  &quot;chainName&quot;: &quot;sol&quot;
}</code></div></pre>
<hr/>
<h1>5. Response (Contains PASETO Token)</h1>
<p>Example:</p>
<pre><div node="[object Object]" style="background:hsl(220, 13%, 18%);color:hsl(220, 14%, 71%);text-shadow:0 1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3);font-family:&quot;Fira Code&quot;, &quot;Fira Mono&quot;, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;DejaVu Sans Mono&quot;, monospace;direction:ltr;text-align:left;white-space:pre;word-spacing:normal;word-break:normal;line-height:1.5;-moz-tab-size:2;-o-tab-size:2;tab-size:2;-webkit-hyphens:none;-moz-hyphens:none;-ms-hyphens:none;hyphens:none;padding:1em;margin:0.5em 0;overflow:auto;border-radius:0.3em"><code class="language-json" style="white-space:pre;background:hsl(220, 13%, 18%);color:hsl(220, 14%, 71%);text-shadow:0 1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3);font-family:&quot;Fira Code&quot;, &quot;Fira Mono&quot;, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;DejaVu Sans Mono&quot;, monospace;direction:ltr;text-align:left;word-spacing:normal;word-break:normal;line-height:1.5;-moz-tab-size:2;-o-tab-size:2;tab-size:2;-webkit-hyphens:none;-moz-hyphens:none;-ms-hyphens:none;hyphens:none">{
  &quot;payload&quot;: {
    &quot;token&quot;: &quot;v2.public.eyJhbGciOiJFZERTQSJ9....&quot;,
    &quot;userId&quot;: &quot;12345&quot;
  }
}</code></div></pre>
<h3>Token format</h3>
<pre><code node="[object Object]">v2.public.&lt;payload&gt;.&lt;signature&gt;
</code></pre>
<p>This is a <strong>PASETO token</strong>.</p>
<hr/>
<h1>6. Store Token (Client)</h1>
<p>Your code stores it in cookies.</p>
<p>Example:</p>
<pre><code node="[object Object]">erebrus_token_evm
erebrus_wallet_evm
erebrus_userid_evm
</code></pre>
<p>or</p>
<pre><code node="[object Object]">erebrus_token_solana
</code></pre>
<p>Token TTL in your client:</p>
<pre><code node="[object Object]">24 hours
</code></pre>
<hr/>
<h1>7. Authenticated Requests</h1>
<p>Future API calls send the token.</p>
<p>Example header:</p>
<pre><code node="[object Object]">Authorization: Bearer &lt;PASETO_TOKEN&gt;
</code></pre>
<hr/>
<h1>8. Complete Authentication Flow (Simple)</h1>
<pre><code node="[object Object]">1. Connect wallet
2. GET /flowid
3. Sign message
4. POST /authenticate
5. Receive PASETO token
6. Store token
7. Use token for API access
</code></pre>
<hr/>
<h1>9. Minimal Authentication Script (Node Example)</h1>
<p>Example without React.</p>
<pre><div node="[object Object]" style="background:hsl(220, 13%, 18%);color:hsl(220, 14%, 71%);text-shadow:0 1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3);font-family:&quot;Fira Code&quot;, &quot;Fira Mono&quot;, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;DejaVu Sans Mono&quot;, monospace;direction:ltr;text-align:left;white-space:pre;word-spacing:normal;word-break:normal;line-height:1.5;-moz-tab-size:2;-o-tab-size:2;tab-size:2;-webkit-hyphens:none;-moz-hyphens:none;-ms-hyphens:none;hyphens:none;padding:1em;margin:0.5em 0;overflow:auto;border-radius:0.3em"><code class="language-javascript" style="white-space:pre;background:hsl(220, 13%, 18%);color:hsl(220, 14%, 71%);text-shadow:0 1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.3);font-family:&quot;Fira Code&quot;, &quot;Fira Mono&quot;, Menlo, Consolas, &quot;DejaVu Sans Mono&quot;, monospace;direction:ltr;text-align:left;word-spacing:normal;word-break:normal;line-height:1.5;-moz-tab-size:2;-o-tab-size:2;tab-size:2;-webkit-hyphens:none;-moz-hyphens:none;-ms-hyphens:none;hyphens:none">import axios from &quot;axios&quot;;
import { ethers } from &quot;ethers&quot;;

const wallet = new ethers.Wallet(PRIVATE_KEY);

async function login() {

 const walletAddress = wallet.address;

 const flow = await axios.get(
   `https://gateway.netsepio.com/api/v1.0/flowid?walletAddress=${walletAddress}&amp;chain=evm`
 );

 const { flowId, eula } = flow.data.payload;

 const message = `${eula}${flowId}`;

 const signature = await wallet.signMessage(message);

 const auth = await axios.post(
   `https://gateway.netsepio.com/api/v1.0/authenticate`,
   {
     chainName: &quot;evm&quot;,
     flowId,
     signature: signature.replace(&quot;0x&quot;,&quot;&quot;),
     walletAddress
   }
 );

 console.log(&quot;PASETO TOKEN:&quot;, auth.data.payload.token);
}

login();</code></div></pre>
<hr/>
<h1>10. Important Security Detail</h1>
<p>The reason this works:</p>
<pre><code node="[object Object]">Wallet signature = identity verification
</code></pre>
<p>Backend verifies:</p>
<pre><code node="[object Object]">signature → wallet address
</code></pre>
<p>Then issues <strong>PASETO token</strong>.</p>

<li><strong>How to decode the PASETO token</strong></li>
<li><strong>How to implement this entire auth server yourself</strong></li>
</ul>
